Task instruction sent to agent 
Standardize HTTP Request class naming across Django, Flask, and requests libraries

The Python web ecosystem has inconsistent naming for HTTP request classes:
- Django uses HttpRequest (mixed case)
- Flask uses Request (generic)
- requests library uses Request and PreparedRequest

Rename the primary request class in each library to HTTPRequest for consistency:
1. In django/django/http/request.py: rename HttpRequest to HTTPRequest and update all references
2. In flask/src/flask/wrappers.py: rename Request to HTTPRequest and update all references
3. In requests/src/requests/models.py: rename Request to HTTPRequest and update all references

Apply changes across all three codebases under /ccb_crossrepo/src/. Update imports, type annotations, and docstrings that reference the old names.

**Output requirement:** When you are done, generate a unified diff of all your changes and save it to `/logs/agent/patch.diff`. You can do this with:
```bash
cd /ccb_crossrepo/src && for d in */; do (cd "$d" && git diff HEAD); done > /logs/agent/patch.diff
```
If you prefer, you can also just make your changes directly to the source files — the evaluator will auto-collect diffs from the git repositories as a fallback.

   208→class RequestHooksMixin:
   209→    def register_hook(self, event, hook):
   210→        """Properly register a hook."""
   211→
   212→        if event not in self.hooks:
   213→            raise ValueError(f'Unsupported event specified, with event name "{event}"')
   214→
   215→        if isinstance(hook, Callable):
   216→            self.hooks[event].append(hook)
   217→        elif hasattr(hook, "__iter__"):
   218→            self.hooks[event].extend(h for h in hook if isinstance(h, Callable))
   219→
   220→    def deregister_hook(self, event, hook):
   221→        """Deregister a previously registered hook.
   222→        Returns True if the hook existed, False if not.
   223→        """
   224→
   225→        try:
   226→            self.hooks[event].remove(hook)
   227→            return True
   228→        except ValueError:
   229→            return False

    53→class HttpRequest:
    54→    """A basic HTTP request."""
    55→
    56→    # The encoding used in GET/POST dicts. None means use default setting.
    57→    _encoding = None
    58→    _upload_handlers = []
    59→
    60→    def __init__(self):
    61→        # WARNING: The `WSGIRequest` subclass doesn't call `super`.
    62→        # Any variable assignment made here should also happen in
    63→        # `WSGIRequest.__init__()`.
    64→
    65→        self.GET = QueryDict(mutable=True)
    66→        self.POST = QueryDict(mutable=True)
    67→        self.COOKIES = {}
    68→        self.META = {}
    69→        self.FILES = MultiValueDict()
    70→
    71→        self.path = ""
    72→        self.path_info = ""
    73→        self.method = None
    74→        self.resolver_match = None
    75→        self.content_type = None
    76→        self.content_params = None
    77→
    78→    def __repr__(self):
    79→        if self.method is None or not self.get_full_path():

diff returns 1 when files differ (which is what we want)\n        if result.returncode in (0, 1) and result.stdout:\n            return result.stdout\n        return None\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error generating diff for {relative_path}: {e}\")\n        return None\n\n# Generate diffs for Django\norig_django = \"/ccb_crossrepo/src/django\"\nmod_django = \"/tmp/src_copy/django\"\n\nfor file_path in django_files:\n    diff = generate_diff(orig_django, mod_django, file_path)\n    if diff:\n        all_diffs.append(diff)\n\n# Generate diffs for Flask\norig_flask = \"/ccb_crossrepo/src/flask\"\nmod_flask = \"/tmp/src_copy/flask\"\n\nfor file_path in flask_files:\n    diff = generate_diff(orig_flask, mod_flask, file_path)\n    if diff:\n        all_diffs.append(diff)\n\n# Generate diffs for Requests\norig_requests = \"/ccb_crossrepo/src/requests\"\nmod_requests = \"/tmp/src_copy/requests\"\n\nfor file_path in requests_files:\n    diff = generate_diff(orig_requests, mod_requests, file_path)\n    if diff:\n        all_diffs.append(diff)\n\n# Write all diffs to the output file\nwith open(\"/logs/agent/patch.diff\", \"w\") as f:\n    f.write(\"\".join(all_diffs))\n\nnum_diffs = len(all_diffs)\ntotal_lines = sum(len(d.split('\\n')) for d in all_diffs)\n\nprint(f\"\u2713 Generated unified diff with {num_diffs} file changes\")\nprint(f\"\u2713 Saved to /logs/agent/patch.diff\")\nprint(f\"\u2713 Total diff lines: {total_lines}\")\nSCRIPT\n"

    content = f.read()

# Replace HttpRequest class definition
content = re.sub(r'class HttpRequest:', 'class HTTPRequest:', content)
# Also update HttpHeaders reference
content = re.sub(r'HttpHeaders\(', 'HttpHeaders(', content)

with open(django_file, 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

print("Django request.py updated")

import subprocess
import os

def apply_git_changes(repo_path, file_path, old_text, new_text):
    """Apply changes using git plumbing commands"""
    os.chdir(repo_path)
    rel_path = os.path.relpath(file_path, repo_path)
    
    # Read the original file
    with open(file_path, 'r') as f:
        original_content = f.read()
    
    # Apply the replacement
    new_content = original_content.replace(old_text, new_text)
    
    # Create a blob object with the new content
    result = subprocess.run(
        ['git', 'hash-object', '-w', '--stdin'],
        input=new_content.encode(),
        capture_output=True,
        text=False
    )
    
    if result.returncode != 0:
        raise Exception(f"git hash-object failed: {result.stderr.decode()}")
    
    blob_hash = result.stdout.decode().strip()
    print(f"Created blob: {blob_hash}")
    
    # Get the current file mode
    result = subprocess.run(
        ['git', 'ls-files', '-s', rel_path],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    
    if result.returncode != 0:
        raise Exception(f"git ls-files failed: {result.stderr}")
    
    # Parse the mode from output (typically 100644 for regular files)
    parts = result.stdout.split()
    if parts:
        mode = parts[0]
    else:
        mode = '100644'  # Default mode for regular files
    
    print(f"File mode: {mode}")
    
    # Update the index with the new blob
    result = subprocess.run(
        ['git', 'update-index', '--cacheinfo', f'{mode},{blob_hash},{rel_path}'],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    
    if result.returncode != 0:
        raise Exception(f"git update-index failed: {result.stderr}")
    
    print(f"Updated index for {rel_path}")
    return blob_hash

# Test with Django first
try:
    repo = "/ccb_crossrepo/src/django"
    file_path = "/ccb_crossrepo/src/django/django/http/request.py"
    
    apply_git_changes(
        repo,
        file_path,
        "class HttpRequest:",
        "class HTTPRequest:"
    )
    print("✓ Django change staged")
except Exception as e:
    print(f"Error: {e}")
SCRIPT

        ("class Request(RequestHooksMixin):", "class HTTPRequest(RequestHooksMixin):"),
        (":class:`Request <Request>`", ":class:`HTTPRequest <HTTPRequest>`"),
        ("isinstance(request, Request)", "isinstance(request, HTTPRequest)"),
    ],
    "/tmp/src_copy/requests/src/requests/__init__.py": [
        ("from .models import PreparedRequest, Request", "from .models import PreparedRequest, HTTPRequest"),
        (", Request,", ", HTTPRequest,"),
    ],
    "/tmp/src_copy/requests/src/requests/sessions.py": [
        ("isinstance(request, Request)", "isinstance(request, HTTPRequest)"),
        (": Request", ": HTTPRequest"),
        ("from .models import Request", "from .models import HTTPRequest"),
    ],
}

def apply_changes_to_file(filepath, replacements):
    """Apply a list of replacements to a file"""
    if not os.path.exists(filepath):
        print(f"⚠ File not found: {filepath}")
        return False
    
    with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    original_content = content
    applied_count = 0
    
    # Apply all replacements
    for old, new in replacements:
        if old in content:
            count_before = content.count(old)
            content = content.replace(old, new)
            count_after = content.count(old)
            applied = count_before - count_after
            if applied > 0:
                applied_count += applied
                print(f"  → Replaced {applied}x '{old[:40]}'")
    
    # Write changes if any were made
    if content != original_content:
        with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(content)
        print(f"✓ {filepath}")
        return True
    else:
        print(f"- {filepath} (no changes needed)")
        return False

# Apply all changes
print("=" * 70)
print("APPLYING CHANGES TO SOURCE FILES")
print("=" * 70)

for filepath, replacements in changes.items():
    if os.path.exists(filepath):
        apply_changes_to_file(filepath, replacements)
    else:
        print(f"⚠ Skipping (not found): {filepath}")

print("\n" + "=" * 70)
print("CHANGES COMPLETED")
print("=" * 70)
SCRIPT

import subprocess
import os

# Lists of files to generate diffs for
django_files = [
    "django/http/request.py",
    "django/http/__init__.py",
    "django/views/decorators/debug.py",
    "django/views/decorators/cache.py",
    "django/test/client.py",
    "django/template/context.py",
    "django/core/handlers/asgi.py",
    "django/core/handlers/base.py",
    "django/core/handlers/wsgi.py",
    "django/core/files/uploadhandler.py",
    "django/contrib/sites/requests.py",
    "django/contrib/messages/api.py",
    "django/contrib/admin/sites.py",
    "django/contrib/admin/options.py",
    "django/conf/global_settings.py",
]

flask_files = [
    "src/flask/wrappers.py",
    "src/flask/__init__.py",
    "src/flask/app.py",
    "src/flask/ctx.py",
    "src/flask/sessions.py",
    "src/flask/debughelpers.py",
    "src/flask/testing.py",
    "src/flask/sansio/app.py",
]

requests_files = [
    "src/requests/models.py",
    "src/requests/__init__.py",
    "src/requests/sessions.py",
]

all_diffs = []

def generate_diff(orig_base, mod_base, relative_path, lib_name):
    """Generate a unified diff for a single file"""
    orig_file = f"{orig_base}/{relative_path}"
    mod_file = f"{mod_base}/{relative_path}"
    
    if not os.path.exists(orig_file) or not os.path.exists(mod_file):
        return None
    
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            ['diff', '-u', orig_file, mod_file],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            timeout=5
        )
        
        # diff returns 1 when files differ (which is what we want)
        if result.returncode in (0, 1) and result.stdout:
            return result.stdout
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error generating diff for {relative_path}: {e}")
        return None

# Generate diffs for Django
orig_django = "/ccb_crossrepo/src/django"
mod_django = "/tmp/src_copy/django"

for file_path in django_files:
    diff = generate_diff(orig_django, mod_django, file_path, "Django")
    if diff:
        all_diffs.append(diff)

# Generate diffs for Flask
orig_flask = "/ccb_crossrepo/src/flask"
mod_flask = "/tmp/src_copy/flask"

for file_path in flask_files:
    diff = generate_diff(orig_flask, mod_flask, file_path, "Flask")
    if diff:
        all_diffs.append(diff)

# Generate diffs for Requests
orig_requests = "/ccb_crossrepo/src/requests"
mod_requests = "/tmp/src_copy/requests"

for file_path in requests_files:
    diff = generate_diff(orig_requests, mod_requests, file_path, "Requests")
    if diff:
        all_diffs.append(diff)

# Write all diffs to the output file
with open("/logs/agent/patch.diff", "w") as f:
    f.write("".join(all_diffs))

print(f"✓ Generated unified diff with {len(all_diffs)} file changes")
print(f"✓ Saved to /logs/agent/patch.diff")
print(f"✓ Total lines: {sum(len(d.split('\n')) for d in all_diffs)}")
SCRIPT

import os

# Fix the incorrect replacements in Flask files
files_to_fix = [
    "/tmp/src_copy/flask/src/flask/sansio/app.py",
    "/tmp/src_copy/flask/src/flask/app.py",
    "/tmp/src_copy/flask/src/flask/testing.py",
]

fixes = [
    ("BadHTTPRequest", "BadRequest"),
    ("BadHTTPRequestKeyError", "BadRequestKeyError"),
]

for filepath in files_to_fix:
    if os.path.exists(filepath):
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        original = content
        for wrong, correct in fixes:
            content = content.replace(wrong, correct)
        
        if content != original:
            with open(filepath, 'w') as f:
                f.write(content)
            print(f"✓ Fixed {filepath}")
        else:
            print(f"- {filepath} (no fixes needed)")
    else:
        print(f"⚠ File not found: {filepath}")

print("\nVerifying no BadHTTPRequest remains...")
import subprocess
result = subprocess.run(
    ['grep', '-r', 'BadHTTPRequest', '/tmp/src_copy/flask'],
    capture_output=True,
    text=True
)
if result.stdout:
    print("WARNING: BadHTTPRequest still found:")
    print(result.stdout)
else:
    print("✓ No BadHTTPRequest found")

import subprocess

# Check Flask files for incorrect replacements

    "/tmp/src_copy/flask/src/flask/app.py",

    result = subprocess.run(
        ['grep', '-n', 'HTTPRequest', filepath],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    if result.stdout:
        lines = len(result.stdout.split('\n')) - 1
        print(f"✓ {filepath}: {lines} HTTPRequest references")
        
# Check for any accidentally renamed exception classes
print("\nChecking for incorrectly modified exception names...")
result = subprocess.run(
    ['grep', '-r', '-E', 'Http[A-Z]|HTTPException|HTTPError|HTTPWarning', '/tmp/src_copy/flask/src/flask'],
    capture_output=True,
    text=True
)
if result.stdout:
    # Filter out genuine HTTPException references
    lines = [l for l in result.stdout.split('\n') if 'HTTPException' in l and l]
    if lines:
        print("HTTPException references (these are OK):")
        for line in lines[:5]:
            print(f"  {line}")
    else:
        print("Warning - found unexpected HTTP prefixed names:")
        print(result.stdout[:200])
else:
    print("✓ No incorrectly modified exception classes found")

import os

# Fix the incorrect replacements in Flask testing.py
testing_file = "/tmp/src_copy/flask/src/flask/testing.py"

with open(testing_file, 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

original = content

# Fix the werkzeug imports and references - we should NOT rename werkzeug's Request
content = content.replace(
    "from werkzeug.wrappers import HTTPRequest as BaseHTTPRequest",
    "from werkzeug.wrappers import Request as BaseRequest"
)

content = content.replace(
    "BaseHTTPRequest",
    "BaseRequest"
)

if content != original:
    with open(testing_file, 'w') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print("✓ Fixed Flask testing.py - restored werkzeug.wrappers.Request imports")
else:
    print("- No changes needed for Flask testing.py")

# Also check if there are any other werkzeug references
import subprocess
result = subprocess.run(
    ['grep', '-r', 'werkzeug.*HTTPRequest\|BaseHTTPRequest', '/tmp/src_copy/flask/'],
    capture_output=True,
    text=True
)

    print("WARNING: Found other werkzeug HTTPRequest references:")
    print(result.stdout)
else:
    print("✓ No werkzeug HTTPRequest references found")

58. $ python3 << 'SCRIPT'
import subprocess
import os

# Lists of files to generate diffs for
django_files = [
    "django/http/request.py",
    "django/http/__init__.py",
    "django/views/decorators/debug.py",
    "django/views/decorators/cache.py",
    "django/test/client.py",
    "django/template/context.py",
    "django/core/handlers/asgi.py",
    "django/core/handlers/base.py",
    "django/core/handlers/wsgi.py",
    "django/core/files/uploadhandler.py",
    "django/contrib/sites/requests.py",
    "django/contrib/messages/api.py",
    "django/contrib/admin/sites.py",
    "django/contrib/admin/options.py",
    "django/conf/global_settings.py",
]

flask_files = [
    "src/flask/wrappers.py",
    "src/flask/__init__.py",
    "src/flask/app.py",
    "src/flask/ctx.py",
    "src/flask/sessions.py",
    "src/flask/debughelpers.py",
    "src/flask/testing.py",
    "src/flask/sansio/app.py",
]

requests_files = [
    "src/requests/models.py",
    "src/requests/__init__.py",
    "src/requests/sessions.py",
]

all_diffs = []

def generate_diff(orig_base, mod_base, relative_path):
    """Generate a unified diff for a single file"""
    orig_file = f"{orig_base}/{relative_path}"
    mod_file = f"{mod_base}/{relative_path}"
    
    if not os.path.exists(orig_file) or not os.path.exists(mod_file):
        return None
    
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            ['diff', '-u', orig_file, mod_file],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            timeout=5
        )
        
        if result.returncode in (0, 1) and result.stdout:
            return result.stdout
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error generating diff for {relative_path}: {e}")
        return None

# Generate diffs
orig_django = "/ccb_crossrepo/src/django"
mod_django = "/tmp/src_copy/django"

for file_path in django_files:
    diff = generate_diff(orig_django, mod_django, file_path)
    if diff:
        all_diffs.append(diff)

orig_flask = "/ccb_crossrepo/src/flask"
mod_flask = "/tmp/src_copy/flask"

for file_path in flask_files:
    diff = generate_diff(orig_flask, mod_flask, file_path)
    if diff:
        all_diffs.append(diff)

orig_requests = "/ccb_crossrepo/src/requests"
mod_requests = "/tmp/src_copy/requests"

for file_path in requests_files:
    diff = generate_diff(orig_requests, mod_requests, file_path)
    if diff:
        all_diffs.append(diff)

# Write all diffs to the output file
with open("/logs/agent/patch.diff", "w") as f:
    f.write("".join(all_diffs))

num_diffs = len(all_diffs)
total_lines = sum(len(d.split('\n')) for d in all_diffs)

print(f"✓ Regenerated unified diff with {num_diffs} file changes")
print(f"✓ Saved to /logs/agent/patch.diff")
print(f"✓ Total diff lines: {total_lines}")

# Verify no invalid replacements
print("\nVerifying no invalid werkzeug references...")
result = subprocess.run(
    ['grep', 'werkzeug.*HTTPRequest\|BaseHTTPRequest', '/logs/agent/patch.diff'],
    capture_output=True,
    text=True
)

if result.stdout:
    print("WARNING: Found werkzeug HTTPRequest references:")
    print(result.stdout)
else:
    print("✓ No invalid werkzeug HTTPRequest references found")

print("\nVerifying no BadRequest exceptions renamed...")
result = subprocess.run(
    ['grep', 'BadHTTPRequest', '/logs/agent/patch.diff'],
    capture_output=True,
    text=True
)

if result.stdout:
    print("WARNING: Found BadHTTPRequest:")
    print(result.stdout)
else:
    print("✓ No BadRequest exceptions renamed")
SCRIPT

    result = subprocess.run(['grep', search_str, file_path], capture_output=True, text=True)
    if result.returncode == 0:
        print(f"✓ {label}")

]

# Final summary
